<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">достопримечательный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dostoprimečatelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>достопримеча́тельность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dostoprimečátelʹnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достопримечательность.html>достопримеча́тельности</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достопримечательность.html>достопримеча́тельности</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:достопримечательность.html>достопримеча́тельностей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>notable building or place with historical, cultural, or geographical significance</li>
<li>landmark</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">tourism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sight, place of interest</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доступ.html>до́ступ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dóstup</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:доступный.html>досту́пный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dostúpnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)досту́пнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)досту́пней</b>)

<ol><li>accessible, available</li>
<li>simple, comprehensible</li>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:досуг.html>досу́г</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dosúg</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:досужий.html>досу́жий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dosúžij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>leisurely; idle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> caused by idleness, empty; idle</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дотоле.html>дото́ле</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dotóle</span>) <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>

<li>until that temporal point, thereunto</li></ol>

***дотягивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дотягивать.html>дотя́гивать</a> (25702)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дотяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dotjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дотягивать.html>дотя́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dotjágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to draw <i>(up to, as far as)</i>, to drag <i>(to; as far as)</i>, to haul <i>(up to; as far as)</i></li>
<li>to stretch out <i>(to; as far as)</i>, to extend <i>(to; as far as)</i>, to bring <i>(to)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold out <i>(till)</i>, to last out <i>(till)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to while away one's time <i>(till, until)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to live <i>(till)</i>, to live to see, to last out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reach
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотягивать.html>дотя́гивать</a></b> <i>(<a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a>)</i></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>dotjágivatʹ</b> <i>(do)</i></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">to fall short <i>(of)</i></span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотягивать.html>дотя́гивать</a></b> 2 <a href = vnd.unilang:процент.html>проце́нтов</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>пла́на</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>dotjágivatʹ</b> 2 procéntov do plána</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">fall 2 percent short of the target</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to improve, to put right, to brush up, to edit, to touch up</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to delay, to protract, to drag one's feet</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотяну́ть</a> (11685)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>до-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">do-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">dotjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дотягивать.html>дотя́гивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to draw <i>(up to, as far as)</i>, to drag <i>(to; as far as)</i>, to haul <i>(up to; as far as)</i></li>
<li>to stretch out <i>(to; as far as)</i>, to extend <i>(to; as far as)</i>, to bring <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотяну́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:деревня.html>дере́вни</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dorógu <b>dotjanúli</b> do derévni</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the road has been extended as far as the village</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hold out <i>(till)</i>, to last out <i>(till)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотя́нет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>города</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mašína jedvá <b>dotjánet</b> do goroda</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the car will just about hold out till we get to town</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">самолёт <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотяну́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:аэродром.html>аэродро́ма</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">samoljót ne <b>dotjanúl</b> do aerodróma</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the plane didn't make it to the airfield</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to while away one's time <i>(till, until)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ю</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ужин.html>у́жина</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne znáju, kak <b>dotjanútʹ</b> do úžina</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I don't know how to while away my time until dinner</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to live <i>(till)</i>, to live to see, to last out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотя́нет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:утро.html>утра</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on ne <b>dotjánet</b> do utra</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he won't last/live out the night; he won't last till morning</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:победа.html>побе́ды</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>dotjanútʹ</b> do pobédy</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">not to live to see the victory</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:такой.html>таки́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:количество.html>коли́чеством</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еда.html>еды́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>мы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотя́нем</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зимы</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s takím kolíčestvom jedý my ne <b>dotjánem</b> do zimy</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">this amount of food won't last us till winter</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reach</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to improve, to put right, to brush up, to edit, to touch up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:статья.html>статью</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нужный.html>ну́жно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:немного.html>немно́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотяну́ть</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">statʹju núžno nemnógo <b>dotjanútʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">the article needs a touch-up</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to delay, to protract, to drag one's feet
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:дотянуть.html>дотяну́л</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a>) <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>того́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упустить.html>упусти́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>все</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможность.html>возмо́жности</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>dotjanúl</b> (délo) do tovó, što upustíl vse vozmóžnosti</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">he kept putting the matter off till all chances were lost</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тя<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*dъxnǫti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дохнуть.html>дохну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">doxnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ды́хать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to take a breath, to breathe</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to blow (of a wind), to have a (single) blow</li></ol>
